9-32 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 28, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to this event than just the [Top 8](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpind16/top-8-decklists-2016-08-28). Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9th through 32nd place.


The following players scored 39 points (13-2), missing out the Top 8 on tiebreakers. Nevertheless, their record earned them an invitation and airfare to Pro Tour Kaladesh in Honolulu.







#### Ethan Pulchinski's Naya Burn â€“ 9th at GP Indianapolis 2016
